rm -f gsl*.h
HEADERLIST="../gsl*.h ../*/gsl*.h"; \
	for h in $HEADERLIST; do \
	  BASENAME=`basename $h`; \
	  test -r $BASENAME || ln -s $h $BASENAME; \
	done
